<script type="text/javascript">
var marketType = '';
var prefStoredSet = '';// reading from param
var prefZC = '';// reading from param
var speedperkLN = '';
var speedperkLN2 = '';
if (speedperkLN == '' && speedperkLN2 != ''){
speedperkLN = speedperkLN2;
}
var tempLN = getUserCookieValue('SP_REWARDS', 'LN');
if (tempLN != null && tempLN != '') {
speedperkLN = tempLN;
}
var userTYPE = 'G';
var usersID = '-1002';
var markttouch ='';
var enableAutoSetPrefStore = '1';
function setDefaultLocation()
{
var browserLatitude = '';
var browserLongitude = '';
var geolocRequested = true;
var alreadyRequested = false;
setTimeout(
function(){
if (geolocRequested) {
geolocRequested = false;
setPrefStore(browserLatitude,browserLongitude);
alreadyRequested = true;
}
},
11000
);
if (navigator.geolocation) {
navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(position) 
{
geolocRequested = false;
browserLatitude = position.coords.latitude;
browserLongitude = position.coords.longitude;
setPrefStore(browserLatitude,browserLongitude);
}, function(error){
geolocRequested = false;
if(!alreadyRequested)
{
setPrefStore(browserLatitude,browserLongitude);
}
}, {
enableHighAccuracy: true,
timeout: 10000, // Wait 10 seconds
maximumAge: 300000 // Valid for 5 minutes
});
}
j.cookie('STORESET', 'true', { expires: 365 * 35 , path: '/', domain: cookieDomain});
}	
function setPrefStore(browserLatitude,browserLongitude)
{
var prefStoreCmdURL = '/web/' + 'AjaxPrefStoreLocatorCmd?langId=-1&storeId=10151&catalogId=10051' + '&browserLatitude='+ browserLatitude + '&browserLongitude=' + browserLongitude;
var zipCode = '';
j.get(prefStoreCmdURL, function(resp) {
if (resp != null){
resp = jQuery.trim(resp);
var successResp = jQuery.parseJSON(resp);
if (successResp != "null" || successResp != null ){
//j.cookie('PREFSTOREADDRESS', address, { expires: 365 * 35, path: '/', domain: cookieDomain });
var aPrefStore = '';
if (j.cookie('PREFSTOREADDRESS') != null && j.cookie('PREFSTOREADDRESS') != '') {
aPrefStore = j.cookie('PREFSTOREADDRESS');
j('#preferredStoreCookieAddress1').html(aPrefStore);
truncatePrefStoreHeader('#preferredStoreCookieAddress1');
if(typeof successResp.storeMap != 'undefined' && typeof successResp.storeMap.zip != 'undefined' ){
zipCode = successResp.storeMap.zip;
}
// if prodcut display page then reload available stores
var pathArray = window.location.pathname.split('/');
if (/p/.test(pathArray[1])){	
if(zipCode !=''){
zipCode = zipCode.substring(0, 5);
j("#pickupZip").val(zipCode);
j("#refreshStoresForZipPop").trigger('click');
}
}
}
//window.location.reload(true);
}
}
});
}
if((j.cookie('PREFSTORE') == null ||j.cookie('PREFSTORE') == "" ) && (j.cookie('STORESET') == null ||j.cookie('STORESET') == "" ) && enableAutoSetPrefStore == '1')
{
// Get HTML Geolocation and get pref store
setDefaultLocation();
}

			<h1>advanced</h1><span class="snd2" data-snd="en/US/dg/dgdjddstdfshdtd5d5gk"></span><span class=snd2 data-snd="en/UK/dg/dgdjddstdfshdtd5d5gk"></span> <br>Also found in: <a href="http://www.freethesaurus.com/advanced">Thesaurus</a>, <a href="http://medical-dictionary.thefreedictionary.com/advanced">Medical</a>, <a href="http://legal-dictionary.thefreedictionary.com/advanced">Legal</a>, <a href="http://financial-dictionary.thefreedictionary.com/advanced">Financial</a>, <a href="http://acronyms.thefreedictionary.com/advanced">Acronyms</a>, <a href="http://idioms.thefreedictionary.com/advanced">Idioms</a>, <a href="http://encyclopedia2.thefreedictionary.com/advanced">Encyclopedia</a>.
		<div id="MainTxt">
			<div id="Definition"><section data-src="hm"><h2>ad·vanced</h2> <span class="snd" data-snd="A0102000"></span> <span class="pron" onclick="pron_key()">(&#x103;d-v&#x103;nst&#x2032;)</span><div class="pseg"><i>adj.</i><div class="ds-list"><b>1. </b> Highly developed or complex.</div><div class="ds-list"><b>2. </b> Being at a higher level than others: <span class="illustration">an advanced text in physics.</span></div><div class="ds-list"><b>3. </b> Ahead of the times; progressive: <span class="illustration">advanced teaching methods.</span></div><div class="ds-list"><b>4. </b> Far along in course or time: <span class="illustration">an advanced stage of illness; a person of advanced age.</span></div></div></section><section data-src="hc_dict"><h2>advanced</h2> (<span onclick="pron_key(1)" class="pron">ədˈvɑːnst</span>) <div><i>adj</i><div class="ds-list"><b>1. </b>being ahead in development, knowledge, progress, etc: <span class="illustration">advanced studies</span>. </div><div class="ds-list"><b>2. </b>having reached a comparatively late stage: <span class="illustration">a man of advanced age</span>. </div><div class="ds-list"><b>3. </b>ahead of the times: <span class="illustration">advanced views on religion</span>. </div></div></section><section data-src="rHouse"><h2>ad&#8226;vanced</h2> <span onclick="pron_key(1)" class="pron"> (æd&#712;vænst, -&#712;v&#593;nst) </span> <br> <br> <i>adj. </i> <div class="ds-list"> <b> 1. </b> placed ahead or forward: <span class="illustration"> with one foot advanced.</span> </div> <div class="ds-list"> <b> 2. </b> beyond the beginning, elementary, or intermediate: <span class="illustration"> a course in advanced mathematics.</span> </div> <div class="ds-list"> <b> 3. </b> far or further along in progress, development, or growth. </div> <div class="ds-list"> <b> 4. </b> of or embodying modern, enlightened, or liberal ideas: <span class="illustration"> advanced theories of child care.</span> </div> <div class="ds-list"> <b> 5. </b> far along in time: <span class="illustration"> a person of advanced age.</span> </div> <div class="etyseg">[1425&#8211;75]</div> </section></div>
